ReFrame logs

1. ReFrame scheduler script

#!/bin/bash
#SBATCH --job-name="rfm_RegressionTest_ced1a8f0"
#SBATCH --ntasks=3840
#SBATCH --ntasks-per-node=128
#SBATCH --cpus-per-task=1
#SBATCH --output=rfm_job.out
#SBATCH --error=rfm_job.err
#SBATCH --exclusive
#SBATCH --partition=cpu
#SBATCH --threads-per-core=1
#SBATCH --time=0-00:30:0
module load OpenMPI/4.1.5-GCC-12.3.0
srun --cpus-per-task=1 singularity exec -B"/ceph/hpc/home/euvincentc/actions-runner/_work/bench.ktirio.fr/bench.ktirio.fr/build/reframe/stage/vega/cpu/default/RegressionTest_ced1a8f0:/rfm_workdir" --home /exa5/data/d2024d05-047-users/euvincentc/apptainer_home --bind /exa5/data/d2024d05-047-users/euvincentc/inputdataset:/input_data --env OMP_NUM_THREADS=1 --bind /opt:/opt /ceph/hpc/home/euvincentc/images_sif/kub_feature-cem_partitioning-sif feelpp_kub_cem --config-files /input_data/kub/idealHeaters.cfg --cem.simulator.sun.filename=/input_data/kub/simulators/Sun.fmu --cem.simulator.lod0.modelisation.maxfloors=10 --cem.preprocessing.dataregistry.directory=/input_data/kub_benchmark/2km/preprocessing --cem.weather.filename=/input_data/kub/Paris/weather.csv --cem.scenarios.filename=/input_data/kub/scenarios_local/scenarios.json --cem.instance.time.start=0 --cem.instance.time.stop=86400 --cem.instance.time.step=3600 --cem.instance.postprocess.export.visualization.enabled=true --cem.instance.postprocess.export.report.enabled=true --cem.instance.postprocess.export.outputs.csv.enabled=false --cem.instance.postprocess.export.outputs.enabled=true --cem.instance.solar_shading.enabled=true --cem.instance.idealflows.enabled=true --cem.database.directory /exa5/data/d2024d05-047-users/euvincentc/apptainer_home/kub/ced1a8f0/Paris_partitioned --directory /exa5/data/d2024d05-047-users/euvincentc/apptainer_home/kub/ced1a8f0/Paris_partitioned --cem.instance.solar_shading.ray-tracing.quad-order 1
